This place is a haven for those who appreciate natural beauty, as it provides breathtaking views of the mountains, lush forests, and enchanting streams that Zhangjiajie is renowned for. 

But what truly sets this place apart is its exceptional staff. They are not just employees running a hotel; they are true ambassadors of the local culture, offering a warm and genuine welcome to every guest. The staff (special thanks to lovely Akun and Ajie) went above and beyond to ensure our comfort throughout the stay, providing personalized service that was second to none. From the seamless check-in process to the adept recommendations for local sightseeing and dining options, the service was flawless. 

Rooms are comfortable and thoughtfully designed, reflecting the natural beauty of Zhangjiajie. Although we experienced some problems with our shower, it was quickly fixed by the hotel‚Äôs staff. 

I must also commend the culinary experience at the hotel‚Äôs restaurant - a gastronomic delight that truly enhances the overall stay. The food here is nothing short of spectacular, a tasteful fusion of local Zhangjiajie cuisine and international flavours. The breakfast selection is small, compared to those in the big hotels, but it is expected. Although the menu selection isn‚Äôt big, each dish is thoughtfully crafted, showcasing the best of seasonal and locally sourced ingredients.

For anyone planning a trip to Zhangjiajie, I cannot recommend the ANNICA Hotel highly enough. It‚Äôs not just a place to stay - it's a place to experience the spirit of Zhangjiajie.

msg:We are a family of 4 (2 adults, 2 kids both young teenagers) who decided to spend our Christmas holiday in Zhangjiajie.  We were looking for a hotel or inn that could house us all in 1 spacious family suite, conveniently located near the national park, and is more private and quiet for families like us (not the package tour group type of commercial hotel).  We are lucky Ctrip recommended this Annica Inn to us as a first choice.  It was almost a perfect fit.  It's a brand new 'premium' inn, situated 5 minutes walk from Zimugang Gate of the Zhangjiajie National Park.  Our 2 bedroom family suite with balcony was very spacious, very well equipped, and even had floor heating to keep us comfortable in the cold winter night.  The staff were friendly and helpful, especially Ah Jie the Inn keeper.  Ah Jie was super attentive and took very good care of us, helping us purchase tickets in advance, plan our daily routes in the parks, and even driving us to a couple scenic spots.  Overall, we are very pleased with our stay at Annica, and would recommend this place to anybody looking to spend a comfortable and relaxing few days in Zhangjiaje.

However, hotels in the suburbs often have problems with inadequate supporting facilities and service levels. In the end, I chose ANNICA and booked two nights directly. Terrace room package.
Before arriving, I began to feel the enthusiasm of the host. I contacted the hotel in advance to arrange a pick-up. I was amazed by the scenery along the way up the mountain. When I got off the bus and entered the lobby, I saw the infinity pool & the iconic ANNICA logo against the green mountains. Be healed.
From the first ANNICA employee you contact, you can feel that they are different from other hotel/B&B employees. They are full of energy and enthusiasm. They can carefully prepare everything the customer needs before they need it without too many formulaic processes.
On the first night of my stay, I met the owner of the B&B, an interesting soul owner who is strict with himself and lenient towards others, and has both grace and good looks.
We talked about business philosophy, education experience, food, culture and travel, aesthetics, and a lot more. After we finished talking, I learned that ANNICA means incomplete or imperfect in Greek. The boss advised me to accept that I am Imperfect, you are ordinary, it is good to enjoy this imperfection.
But judging from the stay experience, I don‚Äôt think he can accept his imperfections at all. . . He was very involved in satisfying customers and employees. During his stay, he even experienced the boss knocking out the floor-to-ceiling glass in the corridor and replacing it with a switchable floor-to-ceiling window for ventilation. . .
In addition, the hotel chef's skills are extremely good, at least not inferior to the executive chef of Changsha W Hotel who just had a meal a few days ago. He even went back for a meal after checking out and going to Zhangjiajie National Forest Park. The signature fish cooked by the chef is far better than the famous restaurants in the city in terms of taste and heat.
To put it objectively, ANNICA is worthy of being called the number one B&B in Zhangjiajie. Its quality far exceeds that of ordinary B&Bs, adding a perfect experience to the journey that is not inferior to Ritz-Carlton or St. Regis.
To put it mildly, ANNICA is a place that can be regarded as the habitat of the soul, including the boss, chefs, employees, buildings, and scenery.
All in all, I will repurchase indefinitely.

Secondly, the inn‚Äôs service is very meticulous and warm: before check-in, I took the trouble to answer our various questions about travel routes on WeChat, and gave a lot of pertinent suggestions and help; , the boss helped to send to the hospital for examination immediately and contacted to issue a diagnosis certificate to facilitate our air ticket rebooking. I really felt very at ease; the hotel also specially made light home-cooked dishes for the child with weak spleen and stomach, which really made us feel at home.
Once again, the hotel has a store manager who can be called a "living map of Zhangjiajie". Since he likes to travel and hike, he is very familiar with the travel routes in Zhangjiajie Forest Park. Follow his itinerary plan. On the most crowded May Day, we are in the forest The itinerary of the park is like getting a fast pass card, perfectly avoiding the peak of the crowd, and having fun with ease.
If I come to Zhangjiajie again, I will choose to stay in "White City"!
